  <script type="text/javascript">
   var docCookies = {
	storageAvailable : function(){
		try {
			var storage = window.sessionStorage;
			var x = 'teststorage';
			storage.setItem(x, x);
			storage.removeItem(x);
			return true;
		} catch(e) {
			return false;
		}
	}(),
	getItem: function (sKey) {
		if(this.storageAvailable && sKey.indexOf('kmostore') === 0){
			localStorage.getItem(sKey);
		}
		return decodeURIComponent(document.cookie.replace(new RegExp("(?:(?:^|.*;)\\s*" + encodeURIComponent(sKey).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g, "\$&") + "\\s*\\=\\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$"), "$1")) || null;
	},
	setItem: function (sKey, sValue, vEnd, sPath, sDomain, bSecure) {
		if (!sKey || /^(?:expires|max\-age|path|domain|secure)$/i.test(sKey)) { return false; }
		if(this.storageAvailable && sKey.indexOf('kmostore') === 0){
			sessionStorage.setItem(sKey,sValue);
		}
		var sExpires = "";
		if (vEnd) {
			switch (vEnd.constructor) {
			case Number:
				sExpires = vEnd === Infinity ? "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT" : "; max-age=" + vEnd;
				break;
			case String:
				sExpires = "; expires=" + vEnd;
				break;
			case Date:
				sExpires = "; expires=" + vEnd.toUTCString();
				break;
			}
		}
		document.cookie = encodeURIComponent(sKey) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(sValue) + sExpires + (sDomain ? "; domain=" + sDomain : "") + "; path=/" + (bSecure ? "; secure" : "");
		return true;
	},
	removeItem: function (sKey, sPath, sDomain) {
		if(this.storageAvailable && sKey.indexOf('kmostore') === 0){
			sessionStorage.removeItem(sKey);
			return true;
		}
		if (!sKey || !this.hasItem(sKey)) { return false; }
		document.cookie = encodeURIComponent(sKey) + "=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT" + ( sDomain ? "; domain=" + sDomain : "") + "; path=/";
		return true;
	},
	hasItem: function (sKey) {
		if(this.storageAvailable && sKey.indexOf('kmostore') === 0){
			return sessionStorage.getItem(sKey) != null;
		}
		return (new RegExp("(?:^|;\\s*)" + encodeURIComponent(sKey).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g, "\$&") + "\\s*\\=")).test(document.cookie);
	},
	deparam: function (query) {
		var pairs, i, keyValuePair, key, value, map = {};
		if (query !== '' && query !== null) {
			pairs = query.split('&');
			for (i = 0; i < pairs.length; i += 1) {
				keyValuePair = pairs[i].split('=');
				key = keyValuePair[0];
				value = (keyValuePair.length > 1) ? keyValuePair[1] : undefined;
				map[key] = value;
			}
		}
		return map;
	}
};
  </script>

   var sq = (function(){
	var scriptQueue = function(){
		var _queue = [];
		var _queueb4Ready = [];
		var _queueAfterLoad = [];
		return{
			
			processQ:function(){
				if(typeof _queue != "undefined"){
					for (var i = 0; i < _queue.length; i++) { 
						try {
						  _queue[i]();
						} catch(e){console.log(e)};
					}
				}
			},
			
			processQb4Ready:function(){
				if(typeof _queueb4Ready != "undefined"){
					for (var i = 0; i < _queueb4Ready.length; i++) { 
						_queueb4Ready[i]();
					}
				}
			},
			
			processQAfterLoad:function(){
				if(typeof _queueAfterLoad != "undefined"){
					for (var i = 0; i < _queueAfterLoad.length; i++) { 
						_queueAfterLoad[i]();
					}
				}
			},
			
			addToQ:function(val, b4ready){
				if(typeof b4ready != "undefined" && b4ready == true){
					if(typeof _queueb4Ready == "undefined" || _queueb4Ready == null){
						_queueb4Ready = [];
					}
					
					_queueb4Ready.push(val);
				}
				else{
					if(typeof _queue == "undefined" || _queue == null){
						_queue = [];
					}
					
					_queue.push(val);
				}
			},
			addToQAfterLoad:function(val){
				if(typeof _queueAfterLoad == "undefined" || _queueAfterLoad == null){
					_queueAfterLoad = [];
				}
				
				_queueAfterLoad.push(val);
			}
		}
	}
	return new scriptQueue();
})(this);
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var kmo_wcs_pb$ = (function(){
    var returnObject = {};
    var storeData = function(){
        var _storeDataVariables = {};
        var storeDataFunctions = {
        	
            setData: function(props){
            	if(typeof props != "undefined" && typeof props == "object"){
	                for(var key in props){
	                    storeDataFunctions.set(key, props[key]);
	                }
            	}
            },
            
            set: function(name, value){
                _storeDataVariables[name] = value;
                var functionName = "get"+name.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + name.slice(1);
                
                returnObject[functionName] = function(){
                    return _storeDataVariables[name];
                }
                
                storeDataFunctions[functionName] = function(){
                    return _storeDataVariables[name];
                }
            },
            
            get:function(name){
            	return _storeDataVariables[name];
            },
            
            append:function(name, column, value){
            	if(typeof _storeDataVariables[name] == "undefined"){
            		_storeDataVariables[name] = {};
            	}
            	_storeDataVariables[name][column] = value;
            }, 
            
            debug:function(){
                var result = {};
                for(var key in _storeDataVariables){
                    result[key] = storeDataFunctions.get(key);
                }
                return result;
            }
        };
        return storeDataFunctions;
    }

   	var _providedEvent = [];
   	var _eventMap = {}
   	var importFunctions = {
   			require: function(name, func){
   				if(_providedEvent.indexOf(name) > -1){
   					func.call();
   				}
   				if(typeof _eventMap[name] == "undefined"){
   					_eventMap[name] = [];
   				}
   				_eventMap[name].push(func);
   			},
   			provide: function(name){
   				_providedEvent.push(name);
   				if(typeof _eventMap[name] != "undefined"){
   					for(var i = 0; i < _eventMap[name].length; i++) {
   						_eventMap[name][i].call();
   					}
   				}
   			}
   	}

    returnObject.storeData = new storeData();
    returnObject.eventBus = {};
    returnObject.require = importFunctions.require;
    returnObject.provide = importFunctions.provide;
    
    return returnObject;

})();

kmo_wcs_pb$.storeData.setData({
		jsDir:"/staticassets/fashionbrand/js/",
		environment:"production"
});

  <script type="text/javascript">
   (function(){
		
		var loadingScripts = [];
		var loadScript = function(script) {
			loadingScripts.push(script);
			$.ajax({
				method : 'GET',
				url : script,
				dataType : 'text'
			}).done( function(data){
				$.globalEval(data);
				loadingScripts.pop();
				if(loadingScripts.length === 0){
					sq.processQAfterLoad();
				}
			});
		};
		var init = function(){
			var readyFunctions = $('#readyFunctions').html();
			var readyJs;
			
			if(checkDevice.isIE8()){
				readyJs = readyFunctions.slice(4, readyFunctions.length-4);
			} else {
				readyJs = readyFunctions.slice(2, readyFunctions.length-2);
			}
			
			$.globalEval(readyJs);
			
			
		}
		try {
		
				$.getScript('/staticassets/fashionbrand/js/kmo.min.js?2018-07-31-06.40.16.200433',init);
			
		} catch(e) {
			if(window.console){
				console.log(e);
			}
		}
	})();
  </script>

 		}
 	}(),
 	getItem: function (sKey) {
 		if(this.storageAvailable && sKey.indexOf('kmostore') === 0){
 			localStorage.getItem(sKey);
 		}
 		return decodeURIComponent(document.cookie.replace(new RegExp("(?:(?:^|.*;)\\s*" + encodeURIComponent(sKey).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g, "\$&") + "\\s*\\=\\s*([^;]*).*$)|^.*$"), "$1")) || null;
 	},
 	setItem: function (sKey, sValue, vEnd, sPath, sDomain, bSecure) {
 		if (!sKey || /^(?:expires|max\-age|path|domain|secure)$/i.test(sKey)) { return false; }
 		if(this.storageAvailable && sKey.indexOf('kmostore') === 0){
 			sessionStorage.setItem(sKey,sValue);
 		}
 		var sExpires = "";
 		if (vEnd) {
 			switch (vEnd.constructor) {
 			case Number:
 				sExpires = vEnd === Infinity ? "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT" : "; max-age=" + vEnd;
 				break;
 			case String:
 				sExpires = "; expires=" + vEnd;
 				break;
 			case Date:
 				sExpires = "; expires=" + vEnd.toUTCString();
 				break;
 			}
 		}
 		document.cookie = encodeURIComponent(sKey) + "=" + encodeURIComponent(sValue) + sExpires + (sDomain ? "; domain=" + sDomain : "") + "; path=/" + (bSecure ? "; secure" : "");
 		return true;
 	},
 	removeItem: function (sKey, sPath, sDomain) {
 		if(this.storageAvailable && sKey.indexOf('kmostore') === 0){
 			sessionStorage.removeItem(sKey);
 			return true;
 		}
 		if (!sKey || !this.hasItem(sKey)) { return false; }
 		document.cookie = encodeURIComponent(sKey) + "=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT" + ( sDomain ? "; domain=" + sDomain : "") + "; path=/";
 		return true;
 	},
 	hasItem: function (sKey) {
 		if(this.storageAvailable && sKey.indexOf('kmostore') === 0){
 			return sessionStorage.getItem(sKey) != null;
 		}
 		return (new RegExp("(?:^|;\\s*)" + encodeURIComponent(sKey).replace(/[\-\.\+\*]/g, "\$&") + "\\s*\\=")).test(document.cookie);
 	},
 	deparam: function (query) {
 		var pairs, i, keyValuePair, key, value, map = {};
 		if (query !== '' && query !== null) {
 			pairs = query.split('&');
 			for (i = 0; i < pairs.length; i += 1) {
 				keyValuePair = pairs[i].split('=');
 				key = keyValuePair[0];
 				value = (keyValuePair.length > 1) ? keyValuePair[1] : undefined;
 				map[key] = value;
 			}
 		}
 		return map;
 	}
 };
   </script>

 					_queue.push(val);
 				}
 			},
 			addToQAfterLoad:function(val){

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var kmo_wcs_pb$ = (function(){
     var returnObject = {};
     var storeData = function(){
         var _storeDataVariables = {};
         var storeDataFunctions = {
         	
             setData: function(props){
             	if(typeof props != "undefined" && typeof props == "object"){
 	                for(var key in props){
 	                    storeDataFunctions.set(key, props[key]);
 	                }
             	}
             },
             
             set: function(name, value){
                 _storeDataVariables[name] = value;
                 var functionName = "get"+name.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + name.slice(1);
                 
                 returnObject[functionName] = function(){
                     return _storeDataVariables[name];
                 }
                 
                 storeDataFunctions[functionName] = function(){
                     return _storeDataVariables[name];
                 }
             },
             
             get:function(name){
             	return _storeDataVariables[name];
             },
             
             append:function(name, column, value){
             	if(typeof _storeDataVariables[name] == "undefined"){
             		_storeDataVariables[name] = {};
             	}
             	_storeDataVariables[name][column] = value;
             }, 
             
             debug:function(){
                 var result = {};
                 for(var key in _storeDataVariables){
                     result[key] = storeDataFunctions.get(key);
                 }
                 return result;
             }
         };
         return storeDataFunctions;
     }
 
    	var _providedEvent = [];
    	var _eventMap = {}
    	var importFunctions = {
    			require: function(name, func){
    				if(_providedEvent.indexOf(name) > -1){
    					func.call();
    				}
    				if(typeof _eventMap[name] == "undefined"){
    					_eventMap[name] = [];
    				}
    				_eventMap[name].push(func);
    			},
    			provide: function(name){
    				_providedEvent.push(name);
    				if(typeof _eventMap[name] != "undefined"){
    					for(var i = 0; i < _eventMap[name].length; i++) {
    						_eventMap[name][i].call();
    					}
    				}
    			}
    	}
 
     returnObject.storeData = new storeData();
     returnObject.eventBus = {};
     returnObject.require = importFunctions.require;
     returnObject.provide = importFunctions.provide;
     
     return returnObject;
 
 })();

   <script type="text/javascript">
    (function(){
 		
 		var loadingScripts = [];
 		var loadScript = function(script) {
 			loadingScripts.push(script);
 			$.ajax({
 				method : 'GET',
 				url : script,
 				dataType : 'text'
 			}).done( function(data){
 				$.globalEval(data);
 				loadingScripts.pop();
 				if(loadingScripts.length === 0){
 					sq.processQAfterLoad();
 				}
 			});
 		};
 		var init = function(){
 			var readyFunctions = $('#readyFunctions').html();
 			var readyJs;
 			
 			if(checkDevice.isIE8()){
 				readyJs = readyFunctions.slice(4, readyFunctions.length-4);
 			} else {
 				readyJs = readyFunctions.slice(2, readyFunctions.length-2);
 			}
 			
 			$.globalEval(readyJs);
 			
 			
 		}
 		try {
 		
 				$.getScript('/staticassets/fashionbrand/js/kmo.min.js?2018-07-31-06.40.16.200433',init);
 			
 		} catch(e) {
 			if(window.console){
 				console.log(e);
 			}
 		}
 	})();
   </script>
